Yes Responsible unit: Department of Industrial Engineering and Management Course/CS Responsible: Master in Informatics and Computing Engineering Cycles of Study/Courses Acronym No. of Students Study Plan Curricular Years Credits UCN Credits ECTS Contact hours Total Time MIEIC 121 Syllabus since 2009/2010 4 - 6 56 162 Teaching language Suitable for English-speaking students Objectives BACKGROUND This is the only course on Information Systems in MIEIC. For this reason, we want this course to be an introductory Information Systems in Organizations focusing on their role and how the they contribute to the creation of value. SPECIFIC OBJECTIVES / SPECIFIC AIMS The aim of this course to prepare students to understand the role of Information Systems (IS) in organizations and the importance of its alignment with the business strategy. Learning outcomes and competences Interpret, classify and explain: 1) Sales and Procurement Process managed by an ERP; 2) how the IS contributes to the Value Construction in an organization, with a special focus on ERP and with other IS that integrate with the ERP (eg: manufacturing execution system and warehouse management); 3) Technology trends and their impact on enterprise information systems (Cloud Computing, Big Data, the new Internet). Delivering an integration projecto with Primavera ERP. Working method Presencial Pre-requirements (prior knowledge) and co-requirements (common knowledge) N/A Program PRIMAVERA ERP; Sales and Procurement Processes; Software Development of 3rd Party Applications and Integration with PRIMAVERA. INFORMATION SYSTEMS AND ERP: - Information Systems Concepts: What is an Information System? How many types of information systems we have and their role in the company? The information system as a strategic decision. - Introduction to ERP: Understand the concepts behind an ERP system. Visualize ERP as packaged software. Understand the information integration through the ERP system. - Evolution of ERP - ERP Modules: Finance Module. Human Resource Management (HR) Module. Materials Management (MM) Module. Sales and Distribution Module. ERP & Other Information Systems - Shop Floor"

Sim Unidade Respons\u00e1vel: Departamento de Engenharia Inform\u00e1tica Curso/CE Respons\u00e1vel: Mestrado em Engenharia Biom\u00e9dica Ciclos de Estudo/Cursos Sigla N\u00ba de Estudantes Plano de Estudos Anos Curriculares Cr\u00e9ditos UCN Cr\u00e9ditos ECTS Horas de Contacto Horas Totais MEB 11 Plano de estudos oficial 1 - 6 39 162 L\u00edngua de trabalho Portugu\u00eas Obs.: Materiais em Ingl\u00eas Objetivos Esta unidade curricular tem como principal objetivo fornecer o conhecimento e a pr\u00e1tica para o planeamento e desenho de um sistema de informa\u00e7\u00e3o, principalmente na sua vertente de representa\u00e7\u00e3o e organiza\u00e7\u00e3o da informa\u00e7\u00e3o. A compreens\u00e3o e utiliza\u00e7\u00e3o eficiente do modelo relacional de dados e a sua implementa\u00e7\u00e3o num sistema de gest\u00e3o de bases de dados fazem tamb\u00e9m parte dos objetivos. Outro objetivo \u00e9 o conhecimento e a pr\u00e1tica da constru\u00e7\u00e3o de uma interface adequada capaz de facilitar e dar suporte aos processos de neg\u00f3cio subjacentes ao sistema de informa\u00e7\u00e3o. Essa interface dever\u00e1 permitir executar o fluxo de um processo de neg\u00f3cio atrav\u00e9s das opera\u00e7\u00f5es normais de pesquisa, atualiza\u00e7\u00e3o, cria\u00e7\u00e3o e elimina\u00e7\u00e3o de dados do sistema. Resultados de aprendizagem e compet\u00eancias Ap\u00f3s esta unidade curricular, os estudantes dever\u00e3o ser capazes de analisar e modelar processos organizacionais e as suas necessidades em termos de dados e informa\u00e7\u00e3o, devendo tamb\u00e9m desenhar e construir esquemas relacionais eficientes, a partir dos modelos. Outro resultado esperado ser\u00e1 o desenho e implementa\u00e7\u00e3o de uma interface web, usando uma tecnologia de servidor simples, assim como das opera\u00e7\u00f5es sobre a base de dados relacional que implementa o modelo criado e identificado a partir do processo organizacional. Ao completar esta unidade curricular, o estudante deve ser capaz de: Identificar os requisitos de um sistema de informa\u00e7\u00e3o Desenhar o modelo de dados de um sistema de informa\u00e7\u00e3o usando diagramas de classes UML Transformar o modelo UML para o modelo relacional Criar e explorar a base de dados usando um sistema de gest\u00e3o de bases de dados relacional Elaborar interroga\u00e7\u00f5es \u00e0 base de dados em SQL Desenhar a"

Sim Unidade Respons\u00e1vel: Departamento de Engenharia Inform\u00e1tica Curso/CE Respons\u00e1vel: Mestrado em Engenharia Eletrot\u00e9cnica e de Computadores Ciclos de Estudo/Cursos Sigla N\u00ba de Estudantes Plano de Estudos Anos Curriculares Cr\u00e9ditos UCN Cr\u00e9ditos ECTS Horas de Contacto Horas Totais M.EEC 37 Plano de Estudos Oficial 1 - 6 39 L\u00edngua de trabalho Portugu\u00eas - Suitable for English-speaking students Objetivos Saber analisar, conceber, implementar e documentar sistemas de informa\u00e7\u00e3o de complexidade moderada utilizando o modelo Sistemas de Gest\u00e3o de Bases de Dados relacionais e conceitos Ind\u00fastria4.0. Saber planear e gerir a implementa\u00e7\u00e3o de um sistema de informa\u00e7\u00e3o por uma equipa de pequena dimens\u00e3o recorrendo a metodologias \u00e1geis. Saber utilizar a linguagem de manipula\u00e7\u00e3o e interroga\u00e7\u00e3o de dados SQL em situa\u00e7\u00f5es de complexidade moderada. Resultados de aprendizagem e compet\u00eancias Ao completar esta unidade curricular, o estudante dever\u00e1 ser capaz de (Learning Outcomes - LO): LO1 - Construir o modelo de dados de um problema de complexidade m\u00e9dia num diagrama de classes UML LO2 - Traduzir de UML para Modelo Relacional (MR) e implementar num Sistema de Gest\u00e3o de Base de Dados Relacional (SGBDR) LO3 - Utilizar a linguagem SQL para criar, interrogar e manipular dados e sua estrutura LO4 - Conhecer os sistemas Ind\u00fastria 4.0 (I4.0), os princ\u00edpios e estrat\u00e9gias fundamentais bem assim como os fluxos de dados horizontais/verticais desde o ch\u00e3o de f\u00e1brica at\u00e9 \u00e0 gest\u00e3o LO5 - Conhecer e saber utilizar tecnologias fundamentais associadas a I4.0 em \u00e1reas tal como rastreabilidade (RFIDs, etc) e acesso a dados (comunica\u00e7\u00f5es industriais entre m\u00e1quinas, etc.) e visualiza\u00e7\u00e3o de dados (smart dashboards, etc) LO6 - Desenvolver aplica\u00e7\u00f5es de complexidade limitada envolvendo manipula\u00e7\u00e3o de dados e os conceitos I4.0. Modo de trabalho Presencial Programa 1. Introdu\u00e7\u00e3o aos Sistemas de Informa\u00e7\u00e3o: 1.1 An\u00e1lise, desenvolvimento e arquiteturas. 1.2 Metodologias de desenvolvimento de sistemas de informa\u00e7\u00e3o. 2. Other ways to authenticate Log in Comuta visibilidade da coluna direita You are in:: Start > Courses/CE or Courses/Cycle of Studies or Programmes/Cycle of Studies > Masters Degree > M:ERSI Main Menu FCUP Portal FCUP Presentation History & Heritage Management Departments Services STUDY Courses Students Applications Enrolment RESEARCH Research Centers Research Projects COMMUNITY Alumni Schools Employability International External Services Search Map of Premises Options Admissions Applications Projects / Dissertations / Theses Teachers Scientific Committee Monitoring Committee Courses Master in Network and Information Systems Engineering Course/CS accredited by the Agency for Assessment and Accreditation of Higher Education (A3ES). Transi\u00e7\u00e3o MERSI: Consultar The Master in Network and Information Systems Engineering aims at the advanced training of particularly qualified professionals for the analysis, planning, installation and administration of complex and distributed data storage, processing, and communication systems, qualified to perform functions of great responsibility and leadership in complex, multidisciplinary contexts and with a focus on innovation, or to proceed to a PhD. The duties that may be performed by a Master in Network and Information Systems Engineering include, for example, the planning of infrastructures for complex computer networks and respective services, the management and administration of cloud systems, the coordination and management of tasks related to software implementation, in-depth analysis of security and risk inherent in the integration of information systems, or the preparation of budgets for the installation, maintenance and updating of computer systems. Programme Structure This 120 ECTS second cycle of studies is organized in two academic years (four semesters). The first year consists of an organized set of semestral courses, corresponding to 60 ECTS, whose successful completion grants a non-degree awarding diploma of specialization in Network and Information Systems Engineering. The second year consists of a dissertation of 48 ECTS of scientific character, original and specially carried out for this purpose, whose public defense will allow obtaining the Master's Degree in Network and Information Systems Engineering, complemented by courses totaling 12 ECTS. The course of study includes seven mandatory courses, six in the scientific field of Computer Science, which provide essential skills for a Network and Information Systems Engineer, and one in the scientific field of Management. Descri\u00e7\u00e3o: O DCC assegura uma forma\u00e7\u00e3o de elevado n\u00edvel cient\u00edfico que possibilita aos seus licenciados, mestres e doutores o acompanhamento aut\u00f3nomo e independente do progresso na \u00e1rea, com incid\u00eancia em \u00e1reas fundamentais, mas nunca perdendo de vista a realiza\u00e7\u00e3o pr\u00e1tica dos conhecimentos e compet\u00eancias adquiridas. As licenciaturas e mestrados da responsabilidade do DCC oferecem um vasto leque de sa\u00eddas profissionais, numa diversidade de setores de atividade como a sa\u00fade, bolsa, banca e servi\u00e7os e no \u00e2mbito de sistemas de informa\u00e7\u00e3o, controlo e gest\u00e3o de sistemas cr\u00edticos, administra\u00e7\u00e3o de sistemas e redes, produ\u00e7\u00e3o de conte\u00fados multim\u00e9dia e Internet. O doutoramento foi tamb\u00e9m uma op\u00e7\u00e3o de v\u00e1rios licenciados, que ocupam atualmente cargos de investiga\u00e7\u00e3o e doc\u00eancia no ensino superior. O Departamento \u00e9 constitu\u00eddo por cerca de 41 docentes doutorados efetivos aos quais acresce um n\u00famero vari\u00e1vel de docentes convidados. O DCC \u00e9 respons\u00e1vel na FCUP pela forma\u00e7\u00e3o na \u00e1rea de Ci\u00eancia de Computadores (ou Inform\u00e1tica) nos 1\u00ba, 2\u00ba e 3\u00ba ciclos de forma\u00e7\u00e3o. O DCC est\u00e1 instalado num edif\u00edcio renovado, com infraestruturas de muito bom n\u00edvel, dispondo de espa\u00e7os espec\u00edficos de apoio \u00e0s aulas e de estudo, 12 laborat\u00f3rios de computadores, dos quais 3 s\u00e3o espec\u00edficos para redes e sistemas e 2 para computa\u00e7\u00e3o gr\u00e1fica e multim\u00e9dia (um total de 200 computadores, todos com Linux e cerca de 80 tamb\u00e9m com Windows). A investiga\u00e7\u00e3o no DCC est\u00e1 centrada nas seguintes \u00e1reas: Algoritmos e Complexidade Computacional, Ci\u00eancia de Dados, Computa\u00e7\u00e3o Paralela, Computa\u00e7\u00e3o Te\u00f3rica e M\u00e9todos Formais, Criptografia e Seguran"

Por este motivo, h\u00e1 uma grande procura de profissionais com forma\u00e7\u00e3o em Engenharia Inform\u00e1tica . Estima-se que, a partir de 2020, cerca de metade das novas vagas de emprego na Europa sejam destinadas a esta \u00e1rea. A Engenharia inform\u00e1tica inclui a conce\u00e7\u00e3o e desenvolvimento de software, sistemas de informa\u00e7\u00e3o, administra\u00e7\u00e3o de redes e seguran\u00e7a e tratamento de dados. Porqu\u00ea escolher esta licenciatura? \u2022 Forma profissionais altamente especializados, sendo um dos cursos com maior taxa de empregabilidade ; \u2022 Foi a primeira licenciatura em Portugal distinguida com a certifica\u00e7\u00e3o de qualidade EUR-ACE da Ordem dos Engenheiros, reconhecida em toda a Europa, Am\u00e9rica Latina e \u00c1sia; \u2022 Tem uma estrutura baseada nas melhores pr\u00e1ticas internacionais (ACM, IEEE e CDIO Initiative); \u2022 O projeto final de curso \u00e9 desenvolvido em ambiente laboral (empresa ou centro de investiga\u00e7\u00e3o) com in\u00fameras oportunidades em organiza\u00e7\u00f5es de refer\u00eancia.     "link": "https://sigarra.up.pt/fcup/en/cur_geral.cur_view?pv_ano_lectivo=2024&pv_curso_id=23181&pv_origem=CUR&pv_tipo_cur_sigla=M",
    "content": "FCUP - Master in Network and Information Systems Engineering ATEN\u00c7\u00c3O: Este site utiliza cookies. Ao navegar no site estar\u00e1 a consentir a sua utiliza\u00e7\u00e3o. Pol\u00edtica de privacidade Go to: Content (tecla de atalho: c) Options (tecla de atalho: o) Main Menu (tecla de atalho: m) Iniciar sess\u00e3o autenticada (tecla de atalho: s) Comuta visibilidade da coluna esquerda Portugu\u00eas help login Did you forget your password? Other ways to authenticate Log in Comuta visibilidade da coluna direita You are in:: Start > Courses/CE or Courses/Cycle of Studies or Programmes/Cycle of Studies > Masters Degree > M:ERSI Main Menu FCUP Portal FCUP Presentation History & Heritage Management Departments Services STUDY Courses Students Applications Enrolment RESEARCH Research Centers Research Projects COMMUNITY Alumni Schools Employability International External Services Search Map of Premises Options Admissions Applications Projects / Dissertations / Theses Teachers Scientific Committee Monitoring Committee Courses Master in Network and Information Systems Engineering Course/CS accredited by the Agency for Assessment and Accreditation of Higher Education (A3ES). Transi\u00e7\u00e3o MERSI: Consultar The Master in Network and Information Systems Engineering aims at the advanced training of particularly qualified professionals for the analysis, planning, installation and administration of complex and distributed data storage, processing, and communication systems, qualified to perform functions of great responsibility and leadership in complex, multidisciplinary contexts and with a focus on innovation, or to proceed to a PhD. The duties that may be performed by a Master in Network and Information Systems Engineering include, for example, the planning of infrastructures for complex computer networks and respective services, the management and administration of cloud systems, the coordination and management of tasks related to software implementation, in-depth analysis of security and risk inherent in the integration of information systems, or the preparation of budgets for the installation, maintenance and updating of computer systems. Programme Structure This 120 ECTS second cycle of studies is organized in two academic years (four semesters). The first year consists of an organized set of semestral courses, corresponding to 60 ECTS, whose successful completion grants a non-degree awarding diploma of specialization in Network and Information Systems Engineering. The second year consists of a dissertation of 48 ECTS of scientific character, original and specially carried out for this purpose, whose public defense will allow obtaining the Master's Degree in Network and Information Systems Engineering, complemented by courses totaling 12 ECTS. The course of study includes seven mandatory courses, six in the scientific field of Computer Science, which provide essential skills for a Network and Information Systems Engineer, and one in the scientific field of Management. Acredita\u00e7\u00e3o pela A3ES O ciclo de estudo encontra-se acreditado pela Ag\u00eancia de Avalia\u00e7\u00e3o e Acredita\u00e7\u00e3o do Ensino Superior (A3ES).Mais informa\u00e7\u00e3o pode ser encontrada nos relat\u00f3rios produzidos pela A3ES . S\u00e3o profissionais capazes de estar no topo da hierarquia t\u00e9cnica da ind\u00fastria de software mundial.     "title": "Mestrado em Engenharia de Software - FEUP",
    "link": "https://fe.up.pt/estudar/mesw/",
    "content": "Mestrado em Engenharia de Software - Engenharia na U.Porto Skip to content Pesquisar Home Sobre o curso Testemunhos Plano de Estudos Candidatura Contacto O caminho para a lideran\u00e7a de projetos complexos de Engenharia de Software O caminho para a lideran\u00e7a de projetos complexos de Engenharia de Software Mestrado em engenharia de software Mestrado em Engenharia de Software 2024-02-14T14:09:53+00:00 SOBRE O CURSO O que \u00e9 o Mestrado em Engenharia de Software? O Mestrado em Engenharia de Software \u00e9 um curso de grau acad\u00e9mico que pretende promover a excel\u00eancia na qualifica\u00e7\u00e3o em aspectos nucleares e avan\u00e7ados da Engenharia de Software, desde os seus fundamentos te\u00f3ricos at\u00e9 \u00e0 integra\u00e7\u00e3o de tecnologias inform\u00e1ticas nas organiza\u00e7\u00f5es. A quem se destina este mestrado? O Mestrado em Engenharia de Software (MESW) est\u00e1 projetado para profissionais que buscam atualizar as suas compet\u00eancias, bem como para aqueles que pretendem adquirir novas compet\u00eancias e conhecimentos atuais, ou enveredar em atividades de investiga\u00e7\u00e3o em Engenharia de Software. + Info TEMPO DE DURA\u00c7\u00c3O 2 anos. ESTRUTURA O MESW tem uma componente curricular de 72 ECTS e uma componente de disserta\u00e7\u00e3o de 48 ECTS. OBJECTIVOS GERAIS O Mestrado em Engenharia de Software (MESW) pretende ser um ciclo de forma\u00e7\u00e3o de excel\u00eancia ao n\u00edvel do 2\u00ba ciclo de Bolonha e tem como principal objetivo formar profissionais com s\u00f3lida forma\u00e7\u00e3o de base e compet\u00eancias em Engenharia de Software para suprimir as necessidades do mercado, promover a inova\u00e7\u00e3o e incrementar a competitividade. OBJECTIVOS ESPEC\u00cdFICOS O objetivo do MESW \u00e9 promover a excel\u00eancia da qualifica\u00e7\u00e3o em aspectos avan\u00e7ados e nucleares da Engenharia de Software (ES), desde os seus fundamentos te\u00f3ricos at\u00e9 \u00e0 integra\u00e7\u00e3o de tecnologias inform\u00e1ticas nas organiza\u00e7\u00f5es para que os estudantes possam : Trabalhar eficientemente numa equipa de projeto para desenvolver software de qualidade; Detetar conflitos nos requisitos e definir solu\u00e7\u00f5es nos limites de custo, tempo, conhecimentos existentes e idiossincrasias organizacionais; Projetar solu\u00e7\u00f5es de Engenharia de Software atendendo a restri\u00e7\u00f5es \u00e9ticas, sociais, legais, tecnol\u00f3gicas e econ\u00f3micas; Compreender e valorizar a an\u00e1lise de viabilidade, negocia\u00e7\u00e3o, h\u00e1bitos de trabalho eficientes, lideran\u00e7a, comunica\u00e7\u00e3o e estudo continuado; Aprender novos modelos, t\u00e9cnicas e tecnologias de desenvolvimento de software; Analisar os pontos fortes e fracos da tecnologia de desenvolvimento de software, fomentando a mudan\u00e7a nas organiza\u00e7\u00f5es; Liderar o trabalho em v\u00e1rias \u00e1reas do desenvolvimento de software. PROPOSTA CURRICULAR A proposta curricular do Mestrado em Engenharia de Software segue os princ\u00edpios expressos do Processo de Bolonha, tendo em considera\u00e7\u00e3o os objetivos globais e as altera\u00e7\u00f5es pedag\u00f3gicas dele decorrentes. ACREDITA\u00c7\u00d5ES O ciclo de estudo encontra-se acreditado pela Ag\u00eancia de Avalia\u00e7\u00e3o e Acredita\u00e7\u00e3o do Ensino Superior (A3ES). Mais informa\u00e7\u00e3o pode ser encontrada nos relat\u00f3rios produzidos pela A3ES. \u2013 Info Sa\u00eddas P"

Notice You can find current training opportunities on the central job market de Our traineeships at a glance Expand all entries Biology laboratory technician Biology laboratory assistant Image: Anne G\u00fcnther Job description Biology laboratory technicians carry out tests on animals, plants and microorganisms and analyse the results. Training content The following knowledge and skills, among others, are taught during practical training: Carrying out microbiological, biochemical, cell culture and botanical work Handling and experiments with animals in the zoological-pharmacological field in compliance with the Animal Welfare Act Carrying out activities in the (subject) area|field of molecular biology and genetic engineering Application of basic chemical-physical and diagnostic methods Application of the latest analytical methods and measurement techniques, as well as handling the microscope Planning, preparation and execution of experiments, as well as analysing and documenting results using laboratory-specific procedures Duration and location of the training programme The training period is 3 \u00bd years. The practical training takes place at the Faculty of Biological Sciences at Friedrich Schiller University Jena. The theoretical knowledge is taught at the vocational school centre in Radebeul. Note: A stay at a boarding school is necessary Requirements Good secondary school leaving certificate, especially in science subjects Interest in natural sciences Careful, precise and responsible way of working Enjoy working with computers and technical equipment Ability to work in a team Contact person for this traineeship Stefanie M\u00fcller-Kr\u00f6ckel Phone: 03641-9 49 00 5 E-mail Chemical laboratory technician Chemielaborantin Image: Anne G\u00fcnther Job description Chemical laboratory technicians carry out and evaluate tests on substances and chemical experiments such as analyses and syntheses. Dieses Format ist aufgrund der aktuellen Entwicklung von auf generativer KI basierenden Anwendungen nicht zu empfehlen. Distanzpr\u00fcfung durch Bild- und Tonverbindung per Videokonferenz abgenommen wird. Technology has developed rapidly in the last few decades alone. The processing of complex information in particular plays an enormous role in today's knowledge society. Would you like to help shape digital transformation? Overseeing complex IT systems and developing new software sounds like an exciting task for you? If so, the Bachelor's programme in \u2018Computer Science\u2019 is perfect for you. Through various hardware and software, computer science manages to transmit data in a matter of seconds and to effortlessly connect people all over the world. Also, you can now easily order a wide variety of goods through countless online shops, for example. During your studies, you will not only learn the basics of information processing and different programming languages ; the focus is also on logical thinking and understanding basic information technology and mathematical problems. Allein in den letzten Jahrzehnten hat sich die Technik rasant weiterentwickelt. Gerade das Verarbeiten von komplexen Informationen spielt in unserer heutigen Wissensgesellschaft eine enorme Rolle. Sie wollen diesen digitalen Wandel mitgestalten? Und das Betreuen von komplexen IT-Systemen und die Entwicklung neuer Software klingt nach einer spannenden Aufgabe f\u00fcr Sie? Dann ist der Bachelorstudiengang \u00bbInformatik\u00ab bestens f\u00fcr Sie geeignet. Mit verschiedener Hard- und Software schafft es die Informatik, Daten in Sekundenschnelle zu \u00fcbermitteln und Menschen auf der ganzen Welt m\u00fchelos miteinander zu verbinden. Auch verschiedenste Waren lassen sich beispielsweise mittlerweile problemlos durch unz\u00e4hlige Online-Shops bestellen. Im Studium lernen Sie nicht nur die Grundlagen der Informationsverarbeitung und verschiedene Programmiersprachen kennen, sondern im Zentrum stehen vor allem auch das logische Denken sowie das Verstehen grundlegender informat"

Through various hardware and software, computer science manages to transmit data in a matter of seconds and to effortlessly connect people all over the world. Also, you can now easily order a wide variety of goods through countless online shops, for example. During your studies, you will not only learn the basics of information processing and different programming languages ; the focus is also on logical thinking and understanding basic information technology and mathematical problems.     "title": "Qualit\u00e4tssicherung im Bereich von Studium und Lehre",
    "link": "https://www.rewi.uni-jena.de/6570/qualitaetssicherung",
    "content": "Qualit\u00e4tssicherung im Bereich von Studium und Lehre Zur Startseite der Universit\u00e4t Jena Rechtswissenschaftliche Fakult\u00e4t Zur Hauptnavigation Zum Inhalt springen Zum Fu\u00dfbereich springen Schnelleinstieg Suche Barrierefreiheit Erkl\u00e4rung zur Barrierefreiheit Leichte Sprache Geb\u00e4rdensprache Login Schnelleinstieg Barrierefreiheit Erkl\u00e4rung zur Barrierefreiheit Leichte Sprache Geb\u00e4rdensprache Weitere Eintr\u00e4ge Suche Login Prim\u00e4re Navigation Prim\u00e4re Navigation Fakult\u00e4t Studieninteressierte Studium Internationales Examensvorbereitung Forschung Zur Ebene 1 Zur Ebene 2 Fakult\u00e4t Unterseiten des Navigationspunktes Fakult\u00e4t Qualit\u00e4tssicherung Jura in Jena Fakult\u00e4t Qualit\u00e4tssicherung Qualit\u00e4tssicherung im Bereich von Studium und Lehre Informationen zur Sicherung der Qualit\u00e4t der Studieng\u00e4nge an der Rechtswissenschaftlichen Fakult\u00e4t Campus Foto: Jens Meyer (Universit\u00e4t Jena) Qualit\u00e4tssicherung und Qualit\u00e4tsausbau in Studium und Lehre an der Rechtswissenschaftlichen Fakult\u00e4t erfolgen auf der Grundlage des am 10. Mai 2023 vom Fakult\u00e4tsrat verabschiedeten Konzeptes f\u00fcr die Evaluation von Studium und Lehre der Rechtswissenschaftlichen Fakult\u00e4t der Friedrich-Schiller-Universit\u00e4t Jena . Die Fakult\u00e4t verfolgt das Ziel, ein attraktives, flexibles, konkurrenzf\u00e4higes und zukunftsorientiertes Studienangebot zu erhalten und dieses fortzuentwickeln. Die hohe Qualit\u00e4t von Studium und Lehre in allen Studieng\u00e4ngen der Fakult\u00e4t soll weiter gesichert und ausgebaut werden. Leitgedanken der Qualit\u00e4tssicherung Alle Eintr\u00e4ge erweitern Gewinnung aussagekr\u00e4ftiger Informationen zu den einzelnen Studienprogrammen Zentrale Bedeutung f\u00fcr die Qualit\u00e4tssicherung hat die Gewinnung von aussagekr\u00e4ftigen Informationen zu den einzelnen Studieng\u00e4ngen. Dies umfasst insbesondere Informationen \u00fcber die Studienabl\u00e4ufe, die Studienbedingungen, die Studierbarkeit, die Studieninhalte sowie die Studienorganisation in den einzelnen Studieng\u00e4ngen. Neben einer systematischen Informationsgewinnung, die insbesondere auf regelm\u00e4\u00dfigen Befragungen beruht, sind flexible Formate vorgesehen, um auch individuelle Anregungen, R\u00fcckmeldungen und Erfahrungen von Studierenden und Lehrenden sowie aus der Berufspraxis in den Prozess der Qualit\u00e4tssicherung einzubeziehen. Detaillierte und umfassende Analysen aller Studienprogramme Die gewonnenen Informationen sollen der Fakult\u00e4t eine detaillierte und umfassende Analyse ihres gesamten Studienprogramms sowie der einzelnen Studieng\u00e4nge er\u00f6ffnen. M\u00f6gliche Bedarfe f\u00fcr eine Anpassung und Fortentwicklung der Studieng\u00e4nge sollen ebenso identifiziert werden k\u00f6nnen wie etwaige Schwierigkeiten oder systematische Probleme. Strukturierte Auswertung der gewonnenen Ergebnisse innerhalb der Fakult\u00e4t Die gewonnenen Erkenntnisse werden innerhalb der Fakult\u00e4t strukturiert ausgewertet . Diese Auswertung soll es erm\u00f6glichen, die erforderlichen Ma\u00dfnahmen zur Anpassung und Fortentwicklung der Studieng\u00e4nge sowie zur Beseitigung etwaiger Problembereiche zu erarbeiten und umzusetzen. Hierbei stellt die"

Allein in den letzten Jahrzehnten hat sich die Technik rasant weiterentwickelt. Gerade das Verarbeiten von komplexen Informationen spielt in unserer heutigen Wissensgesellschaft eine enorme Rolle. Sie wollen diesen digitalen Wandel mitgestalten? Und das Betreuen von komplexen IT-Systemen und die Entwicklung neuer Software klingt nach einer spannenden Aufgabe f\u00fcr Sie? Dann ist der Bachelorstudiengang \u00bbInformatik\u00ab bestens f\u00fcr Sie geeignet. Mit verschiedener Hard- und Software schafft es die Informatik, Daten in Sekundenschnelle zu \u00fcbermitteln und Menschen auf der ganzen Welt m\u00fchelos miteinander zu verbinden. Auch verschiedenste Waren lassen sich beispielsweise mittlerweile problemlos durch unz\u00e4hlige Online-Shops bestellen. Im Studium lernen Sie nicht nur die Grundlagen der Informationsverarbeitung und verschiedene Programmiersprachen kennen, sondern im Zentrum stehen vor allem auch das logische Denken sowie das Verstehen grundlegender informat"

Notice You can find current training opportunities on the central job market de Our traineeships at a glance Expand all entries Biology laboratory technician Biology laboratory assistant Image: Anne G\u00fcnther Job description Biology laboratory technicians carry out tests on animals, plants and microorganisms and analyse the results. Training content The following knowledge and skills, among others, are taught during practical training: Carrying out microbiological, biochemical, cell culture and botanical work Handling and experiments with animals in the zoological-pharmacological field in compliance with the Animal Welfare Act Carrying out activities in the (subject) area|field of molecular biology and genetic engineering Application of basic chemical-physical and diagnostic methods Application of the latest analytical methods and measurement techniques, as well as handling the microscope Planning, preparation and execution of experiments, as well as analysing and documenting results using laboratory-specific procedures Duration and location of the training programme The training period is 3 \u00bd years. The practical training takes place at the Faculty of Biological Sciences at Friedrich Schiller University Jena. The theoretical knowledge is taught at the vocational school centre in Radebeul. Note: A stay at a boarding school is necessary Requirements Good secondary school leaving certificate, especially in science subjects Interest in natural sciences Careful, precise and responsible way of working Enjoy working with computers and technical equipment Ability to work in a team Contact person for this traineeship Stefanie M\u00fcller-Kr\u00f6ckel Phone: 03641-9 49 00 5 E-mail Chemical laboratory technician Chemielaborantin Image: Anne G\u00fcnther Job description Chemical laboratory technicians carry out and evaluate tests on substances and chemical experiments such as analyses and syntheses.     "title": "Part-time studies",
    "link": "https://www.uni-jena.de/en/610/part-time-studies",
    "content": "Part-time studies Main page of University of Jena To main navigation Skip to content Skip to footer Quick start Search de Accessibility Accessibility Statement Login Quick start Accessibility Accessibility Statement More entries de Search Login primary navigation primary navigation University Research Studies Academic Career International To level 1 To level 2 To level 3 To level 4 Studies Subpages of the navigation point Studies During your studies Subpages of the navigation point During your studies Organizing your studies Subpages of the navigation point Organizing your studies Part-time studies Home Studies During your studies Organizing your studies Part-time studies Part-time studies Studies at half the speed student in the lecture hall Image: stock.adobe.com Organize your own part-time study Family obligations, working 15 hours per week, illness, and top-level sports are life circumstances and activities that limit the amount of time available to study. It is therefore possible to complete a study programme as a part-time course in many fields of study at our university. For rules on part-time studies, please refer to specific study and examination regulations. The main feature of part-time studies is that you attend the same courses as full-time students, but do not have to pass as many as they are expected to. As a result, this type of studies is mainly suitable for applicants who work or live in Jena or its direct surroundings, and also want to stay flexible regarding their work-life balance. For study programmes enabling part-time studies and corresponding information, please click here . Information Part time studies cannot be funded a German student loan (\u201cBAf\u00f6G\u201d)! For further information, please contact the competent point of contact at the student services organization Studierendenwerk . Expand all entries Who can request a change to part-time studies? Provided that your field of study allows it, you may apply for part-time studies. Typical reasons may be family duties or a job between 20 and 30 working hours. In addition, illness or professional sport can also be recognized as reasons justifying part-time studies. Applications and documentation The application for changing to part-time studies or returning to a full-time study programme can be found here. Please fill in the form and submit it to the Student Service Centre , including supporting documents providing the reasons for part-time studies. Such documents may include a contract of employment, a medical certificate or the birth certificate of a new family member. Deadlines The application must be submitted by 15 September for a winter semester and by 15 March for a summer semester. Please submit your application in full, including the evidence highlighting the reason for wanting part-time study, to the Student Service Centre. To start and complete your enrolment, follow steps 1-7 in the same chapter. When should I transfer my semester contribution? Please make the transfer only after arrival in Jena. See step 3A in the chapter Enrolment . Which health insurance should I mention in my application for enrolment? If you have not got a German statutory health insurance yet, please enter no data. Please see more on this in #2 in the chapter Before Arrival and step 3C in the chapter Enrolment . Has my application for enrolment been received? Please check the status in our application portal External link . Can I enroll (pay the semester contribution) or study online or from outside Germany? No, this is not possible. Please read all about the Enrolment below. Can I get an enrolment certificate for my visa application? No, please use your admission letter for the visa application, An enrolment certificate is issued only after enrolment has been completed, see steps 1-7 below . Which official contact person should I mention in my visa application?     "title": "Qualit\u00e4tssicherung",
    "link": "https://www.wiwi.uni-jena.de/430/qualitaetssicherung",
    "content": "Qualit\u00e4tssicherung Zur Startseite der Universit\u00e4t Jena Wirtschaftswissenschaftliche Fakult\u00e4t Zur Hauptnavigation Zum Inhalt springen Zum Fu\u00dfbereich springen Schnelleinstieg Suche Barrierefreiheit Erkl\u00e4rung zur Barrierefreiheit Leichte Sprache Geb\u00e4rdensprache Login Schnelleinstieg Barrierefreiheit Erkl\u00e4rung zur Barrierefreiheit Leichte Sprache Geb\u00e4rdensprache Weitere Eintr\u00e4ge Suche Login Prim\u00e4re Navigation Prim\u00e4re Navigation Fakult\u00e4t Studieninteressierte Studierende Wissenschaftliche Karriere Forschung Zur Ebene 1 Zur Ebene 2 Fakult\u00e4t Unterseiten des Navigationspunktes Fakult\u00e4t Qualit\u00e4tssicherung Startseite Fakult\u00e4t Qualit\u00e4tssicherung Qualit\u00e4tssicherung Jena Skyline 2 Foto: gemeinfrei nach Creative Commons CC0 Die Qualit\u00e4tssicherung an der Fakult\u00e4t Qualit\u00e4tssicherungsinstrumente Foto: Anna Scheer Studienqualit\u00e4t Mit ihrem Qualit\u00e4tssicherungssystem verfolgt die Wirtschaftswissenschaftliche Fakult\u00e4t mehrere zentrale Leitideen. Insbesondere ist die Fakult\u00e4t bestrebt, ein attraktives und flexibles Studienangebot zu schaffen, bei dem Studierende im Rahmen eines eigenverantwortlichen Studiums Wahlm\u00f6glichkeiten wahrnehmen k\u00f6nnen und, bei einem st\u00e4ndigen Unterst\u00fctzungsangebot durch Studienberatung und Pr\u00fcfungsamt sowie weiteren verantwortlichen Stellen, ihr Studium selbst organisieren k\u00f6nnen. Hierbei richtet sich das Angebot der Fakult\u00e4t an einem zunehmend differenzierten und spezialisierten Arbeitsmarkt aus und wird nach Bedarf entsprechend erg\u00e4nzt (z.B. Einf\u00fchrung mathematisch-quantitativer Studienprofile und Studienprofile im Bereich Wirtschaftsinformatik sowie die Schaffung des Studienganges Wirtschaft und Sprachen, der gezielt auf die stark gestiegene Internationalisierung der Wirtschaft vorbereitet). Die Studierbarkeit der einzelnen Studienangebote ist immer ein zentrales Anliegen, das durch den systematischen Einsatz von Qualit\u00e4tssicherungsinstrumenten erreicht wird. Anlaufstellen f\u00fcr Studierende Studienberatung, Studiengangverantwortliche und Fachschaftsrat sind bei Problemen im Studienablauf oder organisatorischen Belangen Schnittstellen zu den Entscheidungsgremien (siehe Abbildung). Sie tragen Probleme und Verbesserungsvorschl\u00e4ge gezielt in den passenden Entscheidungsprozess. Die Studieng\u00e4nge und -bedingungen sollen in einem kontinuierlichen Verbesserungsprozess \u00fcberpr\u00fcft und ggf. kurzfristig verbessert werden. Studienberatung Das B\u00fcro des Studien- und Praktikantenamtes bietet eine t\u00e4gliche Sprechstunde f\u00fcr Studierende an und ist die erste Anlaufstelle f\u00fcr Fragen zu Studienablauf, Studienorganisation und studienbegleitenden Praktika. Hier werden insbesondere individuelle Anliegen der Studierenden besprochen \u2013 diese sind unterschiedlicher Natur, wie z.B. M\u00f6glichkeiten der Anerkennung bei einem Wechsel von einer anderen Universit\u00e4t an die Friedrich-Schiller-Universit\u00e4t, bis hin zu Fragen bez\u00fcglich der Schwerpunktwahl oder Urlaubssemestern. In den F\u00e4llen, in denen sich systematische Probleme im Studium identifizieren lassen, die \u00fcber individuelle A"

Teilnehmer:innen des Zertifikatsprogramms werden bei der Einschreibung in die Kurse bevorzugt ber\u00fccksichtigt. Von einer wissenschaftlichen F\u00fchrungspers\u00f6nlichkeit wird Kommunikations-, Management- und F\u00fchrungskompetenz erwartet. Sie braucht f\u00fcr ihre Aufgaben Weitblick, Verantwortungsbewusstsein und die F\u00e4higkeit zur f\u00e4cher\u00fcbergreifenden Zusammenarbeit. Um diese F\u00e4higkeiten weiter zu entwickeln, bietet die Graduierten-Akademie das Zertifikatsprogramm \"F\u00fchrung in der Wissenschaft\". Gleichzeitig sind sie in der Lage, interkulturelle Perspektiven in den Konfliktl\u00f6seprozess zu integrieren und somit auf die Komplexit\u00e4t von Konfliktkonstellationen zu reagieren. Mehr erfahren Externer Link Lasertechnik Ziel des Studiums ist ein Abschluss mit Entscheidungskompetenzen im Bereich Lasertechnik / Lasereinsatz. Das Studium vermittelt zun\u00e4chst Grundlagenkenntnisse der Lasertechnik, Lasermaterialbearbeitung und Lasermesstechnik.     "content": "2. semester - University of Ljubljana, Slovenia - Courses and modules - Programme info - Home Master Tribos European Commision Intro entry-text Locations entry slogan Consortium Partners Associated Partners Supporting Partners footer text Programme info Teaching Staff Learning outcome Courses and modules Master degree Projects and Thesis Application info Admission criteria Required documents Application and selection procedure Important dates Selection criteria Participation costs Scholarship possibilities Erasmus Mundus scholarships Other scholarships VISA Insurance Appeal procedure Apply here Alumni Contacts News and events Visiting scholars Gallery FAQ Partner area Programme evaluation Consortium meeting Vodilne fotografije Credits Instagram Twitter Facebook Home | Programme info | Courses and modules | 2. semester - University of Ljubljana, Slovenia Maintenance technologies Maintenance technologies is a 2nd semester course held at University of Ljubljana, Slovenia. Semester 2. semester - University of Ljubljana, Slovenia Lecturer Assistant Prof. Dr. Marko Polajnar, Prof. Dr. Mitjan Kalin Course Points (ECTS) 6.0 Contact Information University of Ljubljana, SLO Course Overview Module objectives The students are acquainted with the activities and the duties of the maintenance department, above all in large companies, and are qualified to participate therein, mainly in the boundaries of EU (unification of concepts, terms). They also learn the physical-technical foundations important for the maintenance activity. Knowledge outcome The students obtain fundamental knowledge for professional management of maintenance work in the company, both for the corrective maintenance and especially for the preventive maintenance on all levels. They also gain the fundamental knowledge necessary to participate and collaborate in investment projects for the field of machinery. Outline syllabus Definitions and terms in the field of maintenance activity, all 11 chapters according to EN 13306. Fundamental and additional duties of the maintenance department. Organizational forms of maintenance department. Maintenance work preparation (organization, duties, responsibilities). Planning and scheduling maintenance work and activity. 8 criterions of tribomechanical system stability according to Fitch. Overview of some typical technical-technological procedures in scope of maintenance activity (vibration, balancing, internal tightness of hydraulic systems (wear), fault diagnostics ...). Planning and designing machines/plants for maintenance and maintainability; general principles of maintainability The relation of maintenance profession to the availability of work means Technical diagnostics in the maintenance activity Ensuring and controlling the proper machine/plant operating parameters and characteristics The relation corrective vs. preventive maintenance; explanation of relations, maintenance tree structure, optimizing condition-based maintenance The effect of maintena"

    "title": "Aplikativna elektrotehnika - Fakulteta za elektrotehniko - UNI-Lj",
    "link": "https://fe.uni-lj.si/studij/dodiplomski-studij/aplikativna-elektrotehnika/",
    "content": "Aplikativna elektrotehnika - Fakulteta za elektrotehniko Sko\u010di na vsebino Za zaposlene Za partnerje Za mlade Vstop \u0161tudent sl en \u0160tudij Raziskovanje Ob \u0161tudiju Knji\u017enica Aktualno O fakulteti Domov \u0160tudij Dodiplomski \u0161tudij Aplikativna elektrotehnika Aplikativna Elektrotehnika visoko\u0161olski strokovni \u0161tudijski program 1. stopnje Avtomatika Elektronika Energetska tehnika in avtomatizacija postrojev Informacijsko komunikacijske tehnologije Tehni\u0161ka kakovost Meni Aplikativna elektrotehnika Vpisni pogoji Vpis v \u0161tudij Predmetnik Pogoji za napredovanje in dokon\u010danje Prakti\u010dno usposabljanje Vzemi prihodnost v svoje \u017ei\u010dke! Visoko\u0161olski \u0161tudijski program Aplikativna elektrotehnika zajema temeljna strokovna in aplikativna elektrotehni\u0161ka znanja ter programerska orodja za delo na realnih elektrotehni\u0161kih problemih. \u0160iroka izbirnost znotraj \u0161tudijskega programa \u0161tudentu omogo\u010di zgodnjo usmeritev v izbrano podro\u010dje elektrotehnike, s prakti\u010dnim znanjem in izku\u0161njami, pridobljenimi ob re\u0161evanju aktualnih izzivov v podjetjih, pa se strokovno usposobi za takoj\u0161en vstop na trg dela. Kako poteka \u0161tudij? \u0160tudij traja 3 leta oziroma 6 semestrov in je vreden 180 kreditnih to\u010dk (ECTS). Prvi letnik \u0161tudija poteka po enotnem predmetniku, v drugem letniku pa se \u0161tudentje usmerijo v eno od petih \u0161tudijskih smeri (Avtomatika, Elektronika, Energetska tehnika in avtomatizacija postrojev, Tehni\u0161ka kakovost, Informacijsko komunikacijske tehnologije). V zadnjem, 6. semestru \u0161tudija, \u0161tudent opravi trimese\u010dno prakti\u010dno usposabljanje ter diplomsko delo. Po opravljeni diplomi \u0161tudent pridobi naziv diplomirani in\u017eenir elektrotehnike (VS) ali diplomirana in\u017eenirka elektrotehnike (VS). Kak\u0161ni so temeljni cilji programa? Temeljni cilj univerzitetnega programa Elektrotehnika je \u0161tudentom zagotoviti: kakovostno aplikativno znanje s podro\u010dja elektrotehnike, sistemsko znanje, potrebno za delo v razli\u010dnih proizvodnih procesih, \u0161tudij v sodobno opremljenih u\u010dilnicah in laboratorijih, mednarodno uveljavljene pedagoge in raziskovalce, interdisciplinarna znanja, ki so uporabna tudi na podro\u010djih medicine, biologije, ekonomije, strojev, ra\u010dunalni\u0161tva, \u0161porta, psihologije in mnogih drugih, prakti\u010dno usposabljanje v podjetju, vseevropsko primerljivost dose\u017eene izobrazbe. Katere kompetence \u0161tudenti pridobijo s programom? Zmo\u017enost definiranja, razumevanja in re\u0161evanja problemov na podro\u010dju elektrotehnike, sposobnost kriti\u010dnega vrednotenja konkretnih re\u0161itev, poklicno, okoljsko in socialno odgovornost, sposobnost strokovnega sporazumevanja v pisni in ustni obliki, sposobnost uporabe informacijsko-komunikacijske tehnologije, sposobnost samostojnega sledenja razvoja stroke, sposobnost timskega dela s strokovnjaki z razli\u010dnih podro\u010dij. Podrobne informacije o \u0161tudiju 1. stopnje APLIKATIVNA ELEKTROTEHNIKA Predstavitveni zbornik Aplikativna elektrotehnika VS Podro\u010dja Aplikativne elektrotehnike Avtomatika Elektronika Energetska tehnika in avtomatizacija postrojev Informacijsko komunikacijske tehnologije Tehni"
